 sitaron kii sabase oonchi manzil par salmaan pahunche
 At a point where Salman Khan's name is enough for films
 box offis par salmaan ke naam par sikkon kii bauchhaar hoti he
 And to achieve all this, Salman also started like a common artist and also worked hard
 filmon ke mashhoor lekhak saleem-javed kii jodi se saleem khan ke ghar main janm hua salmaan khan kaa mumbai main
 In Bandra area of mumbai, they became young like Bandra Boys
 1988 main film 'bivi ho to aisi' se parade par faruq shaikh ke chote bhai banakar aae magar jald hi 1989 main filmkaar suraj badjatya ne salmaan ko parade par naam diya 'prem' kaa or film banaai 'maine pyaar kiya'
 This film became such a big hit that now Salman had become the beat of young hearts
 iske baad 'baagi' or 'pathar ke phool' bhi thik thaak chali or film 'saajan' se salmaan or upar aaye kyonki ye film bhi badi hit ho chuki thi
 But after 'saajan', a bad phase came when 'suryavansham', 'dil Tera Aashiq' and 'jagriti' flopped, then once again Sooraj Barjatya made Salman's love for the screen in 1994 film Hum Aapke Hain Kaun
 In
 ye film aaj bhi bharat kii sabase badi 10 hit filmon main se ek maani jaati he
 The film made Salman Khan a superstar
 uske baad 'andaaz apana apana', 'karan arjuna', 'jeet', 'judawaan' or 'pyaar kiya to darana kya' jaisi safal filmein dekar salmaan 90 ke dashak ke sabase bade sitaron main ek ban chuke the or apane pratidwandiyon aamir khan or shahrukh khan ko box offis par takkar dete hue apane liye alag muqaam bana chuke the
 But the start of the Millennium was not a happy one for Salman
 2000 ke chadhane ke baad film 'ham tumhaare hai sanam', 'har dil jo pyaar karegaa', 'tumko na bhul paaenge' or 'ye he jalawaa' jaisi filmein flop ho gai magar film 'tere naam' se salmaan ne jabardast vaapasi kii
 After this, films like 'garv', 'no Entry', 'mujhse Shaadi Karogi' and 'partner' continued to be big hits
 ek baar phir chota sa phej aayaa jab film 'jane man', 'salaam e ishq' or 'yuvaraj' flop hui magar 2008 main aayi film 'wanted' se salmaan khan kii maano kaaya hi palat gai
 After 'wanted', though the film 'veer' did not succeed, but after this the film 'dabangg' set the example of success which only fortunate people get
 dabang se 100 karod kaa collection paar karne ke baad salmaan khan box offis ke dabang ban gaye or uske baad unki sabhi filmein super hit huin or 100 karod se zyaada kii kamai kii
 After Dabangg all films like 'bodyguard', 'ready', 'dabangg 2', 'jai Ho' and 'ek Tha Tiger' crossed the 100 million mark
 iske baad salmaan ne film 'kik' se box offis par 200 karod kaa aankada bhi paar kar liya
 Now the film 'bajrangi Bhaijaan' is coming and it seems that this film too will cross the 200 crore mark
 salmaan khan kii badi fain folowing ne inhen alag muqaam par khadaa kiya
 Salman did what he did, it became fashion
 jab salmaan ne film 'pyaar kiya to darana kya' main pehali baar shart utari tab filmon main kameez utaarne kaa fishan sa ban gaya
 Salman also gave the youth the impetus to build a good body, and seeing Salman himself, the youth went down to build a body and the trend of gymnasium increased in the country
 salmaan ne jab film 'tere naam' main maathe par gire hue lambey bal rakhe tab yuvaaon ne us hair style ko koob apanaaya
 When Salman called the film Wanted Khan, when the film was called Bodyguard, it was called Bodyguard, when the film was Dabangg, it was called Dabangg Khan
 yani alag-alag filmon se alag-alag tital hasil karte rahe
 Now, since the promos of the film 'bajrangi Bhaijaan' have started, Salman has also been called 'bajrangi Bhaijaan'
 salmaan khan ne apane lambey filmi safar main har tarah kii bhoomikaayen nibhaai
 Made a different place for his own style and made a different place for different types of cool dance
 salmaan khan ne apane parivaar kaa bharpoor khyaal rakhaa
 Made his brothers Arbaaz and Sohail Khan and brother-in-law Atul Agnihotri as producers and directors, who have been almost away from acting
 inaki filmon main salmaan abhinay karte hai or film hit hoti he
 Salman Khan along with his family also helps others a lot
 sangeetkaar himesh reshmia, sajid-waajid ko kaamyaab banane kaa shrey bhi salmaan ko hi jaataa he
 Katrina Kaif and Sonakshi Sinha have also been made by Star Salman
 pichley kuch samay se naakaam rahe nirdeshak suraj badjatya ko nirdesan main vaapasi kaa mauka salmaan de rahe hai film 'prem ratan dhan payo' se
 There are many examples for which Salman stands as a support
 aise main zaahir he ki salmaan ko kisi na kisi kii dua lagegi hi
 The comments salmaan sabhi dharmon kaa sammaan karte hai
 Eid or Diwali, Navratri or Ganapati, celebrate all festivals
 salmaan khan samaaj seva se bhi pichley kai saalon se jude rahe hai
 There is an institution called Being Human through which the poor are supported
 garibon kaa ilaaj karte hai salmaan
 Salman Khan spends a large part of his hard-earned money to help the poor through Being Human
 zaahir he garibon kii awaz or dua sidhe bhagwaan ke paas pahunchati he jiskaa fal salmaan ko mil rahaa he, unki apaar safalata ke naam par
 Salman Khan achieved what he wished in his life, be it stardom, immense success at the box office, big fan following, family love, friends friendship, respect or the blessings of millions of fans
 
 
 vaaki kuch to baat he salmaan main, tabhi to wo sabakaa bhaijan he
 There is something in this person, there is some charisma in his personality, there is some sparkle in his profession which makes Salman the biggest star of Bollywood, everybody makes Bhaijaan
 ek superstar kii haisiyat se salmaan khan ne sab kuch paaya
 Salman reached the highest floor of stars
 aise mukaam par jahaan filmon ke liye salmaan khan kaa naam hi kaafii he
 At the box office, there is a barrage of coins in the name of Salman
 or ye sab kuch hasil karne ke liye salmaan ne bhi aam kalakaar kii tarah hi shuruyaat bhi kii or mehnat bhi
 Salman Khan was born in Mumbai to Salim Khan in the house of salim-javed, a famous writer of films
 mumbai ke bandra ilaake main bandra boij kii tarah jawan hue
 In 1988, Farooq came on screen as the younger brother of Shaikh, from the film 'biwi Ho To Aisi' but soon in 1989, filmmaker Sooraj Barjatya named Salman on screen and made 'maine Pyaar Kiya'
 ye film itani badi hit hui ki ab salmaan yuva dilon kii dhadkan ban chuke the
 After this 'baghi' and 'pathar Ke Phool' also went well and Salman came up from the film 'saajan' because this film was also a big hit
 magar 'saajan' ke baad ek bura daur aayaa jab 'suryavansham', 'dil tera ashiq' or 'jagriti' flop ho gai tab ek baar phir suraj badjatya ne salmaan ko parade par prem banaakar utraa 1994 main film 'ham aapke hai koun' main
 The film is still considered one of the biggest 10 hit films in India
 is film ne salmaan khan ko superstar bana diya
 After that, Salman became one of the biggest stars of the 90s by giving successful films like 'andaz Apna Apna', 'karan Arjun', 'jeet', 'twins' and 'pyar Kiya To Darna Kya' and his rivals Aamir Khan And had made a different place for himself, competing Shahrukh Khan at the box office
 magar milinium kii shuruyaat salmaan ke liye khushgavaar nahin thi
 After the ascension of 2000, films like 'hum Tumhare Hain Sanam', 'har Dil Jo Pyaar Karega', 'tumko Na Bhoolgeon' and 'ye Hai Jalwa' flopped but Salman made a strong comeback with the film 'tere Naam'
 
 iske baad film 'garv', 'no entry', 'mujhase shaadi karogi' or 'partner' jaisi filmein lagaataar badi hit hoti chali gayi
 Once again a small phase came when the films 'jaane Mana', 'salaam e Ishq' and 'yuvraj' flopped, but Salman Khan's body was overturned in the 2008 film 'wanted'
 'wanted' ke baad film 'vir' haalanki safal nahin hui, lekin iske baad film 'dabang' se aisi safalata kii misaal banaai jo kismat waalon ko hi milti he
 After crossing the 100 crore collection from Dabangg, Salman Khan became a box office bully and after that all his films became super hits and grossed over 100 crores
 dabang ke baad 'bodyguard', 'ready', 'dabang2', 'jai ho' or 'ek tha tiger' jaisi sabhi filmon ne 100 karod se zyaada kaa aankada paar kiya
 After this, Salman also crossed the 200 crore mark at the box office with the film 'kick'
 ab film 'bajrangi bhaijan' aa rahi he or aisa lagata he ki ye film bhi 200 karod kaa aankada paar kar legi
 Salman Khan's big fan following made him stand on a different position
 salmaan ne jab-jab jo-jo kiya wo fishan ban gaya
 When Salman landed the shirt for the first time in the film Pyaar Kiya To Darna Kya, it became a fashion to take off the shirt in films
 yuvaaon ko acchhee body banane kaa josh bhi salmaan ne hi diya or salmaan ko hi dekhakar yuva body banane ke liye utar gaye or desh main gymnasium kaa chalan badha
 When Salman had long hair falling on his forehead in the film 'tere Naam', the youth adopted that hairstyle
 salmaan ne jab film wanted kii tab wanted khan kahalaaye, jab film body guard kii tab bodyguard kahalaaye, jab film dabang kii tab dabang khan kehalaae
 That is, they kept getting different titles from different films
 ab jab se film 'bajrangi bhaijan' ke promo shuru hue hai tab se salmaan 'bajrangi bhaijan' bhi kahalaane lage hai
 Salman Khan played all kinds of roles in his long film journey
 apane alag andaaz ke liye alag jagah banaai or alag tarah ke bindaas dance ke liye alag mukaam banaaya
 Salman Khan took great care of his family
 abhinay se kareeb-kareeb dur ho chuke apane bhai arbaz or sohail khan va jija atul agnihotri ko nirmaataa or nirdeshak banaaya
 Salman plays in his films and the film is a hit
 salmaan khan apane parivaar ke saath-saath dusron kii bhi khub sahaayta karte hai
 The credit for making music composer Himesh Reshammiya, sajid-wajid successful also goes to Salman
 katrina kaiff or sonakshi sinha ko bhi star salmaan ne hi banaaya he
 Salman is giving a chance to return to director Suraj Barjatya who has been failing for some time with the film 'prem Ratan Dhan Payo'
 aisi bahut sari misaalen hai jinke liye salmaan sahaara banakar khadey rahete hai
 In such a situation, it is obvious that Salman will have to pray for someone
 tippaniyan Salman respects all religions
 id ho yaa diwaali, navaratri ho yaa ganpati, sabhi tyoharon ko manaate hai
 Salman Khan has also been associated with social service for the last several years
 beeing human naam kii sanstha banaai he jiske dwaara garibon kii sahaayta hoti he
 Salman treats the poor
 apni mehnat kii kamai kaa bada hissaa salmaan khan beeing human ke madhyam se garibon kii sahaayta main lagaate hai
 It is obvious that the voice and blessings of the poor reach God directly, whose fruits are being paid to Salman, in the name of his immense success
 salmaan khan ne apane jivan main jo chaha hasil kiya, phir wo chaahe staradam ho, box offis par apaar safalata ho, badi fain folowing ho, parivaar kaa pyaar ho, doston kii dosti ho, sammaan ho yaa phir lakhon prashansakon kii dua
 
 
 Actually there is something in Salman, that is why he is the brother of all

 Now, since the promos of the film 'bajrangi Bhaijaan' have started, Salman has also been called 'bajrangi Bhaijaan'
 salmaan khan ne apane lambey filmi safar main har tarah kii bhoomikaayen nibhaai
 Made a different place for his own style and made a different place for different types of cool dance
 salmaan khan ne apane parivaar kaa bharpoor khyaal rakhaa
 Made his brothers Arbaaz and Sohail Khan and brother-in-law Atul Agnihotri as producers and directors, who have been almost away from acting
 inaki filmon main salmaan abhinay karte hai or film hit hoti he
 Salman Khan along with his family also helps others a lot
 sangeetkaar himesh reshmia, sajid-waajid ko kaamyaab banane kaa shrey bhi salmaan ko hi jaataa he
 Katrina Kaif and Sonakshi Sinha have also been made by Star Salman
 pichley kuch samay se naakaam rahe nirdeshak suraj badjatya ko nirdesan main vaapasi kaa mauka salmaan de rahe hai film 'prem ratan dhan payo' se
 There are many examples for which Salman stands as a support
 aise main zaahir he ki salmaan ko kisi na kisi kii dua lagegi hi
 The comments salmaan sabhi dharmon kaa sammaan karte hai
 Eid or Diwali, Navratri or Ganapati, celebrate all festivals
 salmaan khan samaaj seva se bhi pichley kai saalon se jude rahe hai
 There is an institution called Being Human through which the poor are supported
 garibon kaa ilaaj karte hai salmaan
 Salman Khan spends a large part of his hard-earned money to help the poor through Being Human
 zaahir he garibon kii awaz or dua sidhe bhagwaan ke paas pahunchati he jiskaa fal salmaan ko mil rahaa he, unki apaar safalata ke naam par
 Salman Khan achieved what he wished in his life, be it stardom, immense success at the box office, big fan following, family love, friends friendship, respect or the blessings of millions of fans
 
 
 vaaki kuch to baat he salmaan main, tabhi to wo sabakaa bhaijan he
 But after 'saajan', a bad phase came when 'suryavansham', 'dil Tera Aashiq' and 'jagriti' flopped, then once again Sooraj Barjatya made Salman's love for the screen in 1994 film Hum Aapke Hain Kaun
 In
 ye film aaj bhi bharat kii sabase badi 10 hit filmon main se ek maani jaati he
 The film made Salman Khan a superstar
 uske baad 'andaaz apana apana', 'karan arjuna', 'jeet', 'judawaan' or 'pyaar kiya to darana kya' jaisi safal filmein dekar salmaan 90 ke dashak ke sabase bade sitaron main ek ban chuke the or apane pratidwandiyon aamir khan or shahrukh khan ko box offis par takkar dete hue apane liye alag muqaam bana chuke the
 But the start of the Millennium was not a happy one for Salman
 2000 ke chadhane ke baad film 'ham tumhaare hai sanam', 'har dil jo pyaar karegaa', 'tumko na bhul paaenge' or 'ye he jalawaa' jaisi filmein flop ho gai magar film 'tere naam' se salmaan ne jabardast vaapasi kii
 After this, films like 'garv', 'no Entry', 'mujhse Shaadi Karogi' and 'partner' continued to be big hits
 ek baar phir chota sa phej aayaa jab film 'jane man', 'salaam e ishq' or 'yuvaraj' flop hui magar 2008 main aayi film 'wanted' se salmaan khan kii maano kaaya hi palat gai
 After 'wanted', though the film 'veer' did not succeed, but after this the film 'dabangg' set the example of success which only fortunate people get
 dabang se 100 karod kaa collection paar karne ke baad salmaan khan box offis ke dabang ban gaye or uske baad unki sabhi filmein super hit huin or 100 karod se zyaada kii kamai kii
 After Dabangg all films like 'bodyguard', 'ready', 'dabangg 2', 'jai Ho' and 'ek Tha Tiger' crossed the 100 million mark
 iske baad salmaan ne film 'kik' se box offis par 200 karod kaa aankada bhi paar kar liya
 Now the film 'bajrangi Bhaijaan' is coming and it seems that this film too will cross the 200 crore mark
 salmaan khan kii badi fain folowing ne inhen alag muqaam par khadaa kiya
 Salman did what he did, it became fashion
 jab salmaan ne film 'pyaar kiya to darana kya' main pehali baar shart utari tab filmon main kameez utaarne kaa fishan sa ban gaya
 Salman also gave the youth the impetus to build a good body, and seeing Salman himself, the youth went down to build a body and the trend of gymnasium increased in the country
 salmaan ne jab film 'tere naam' main maathe par gire hue lambey bal rakhe tab yuvaaon ne us hair style ko koob apanaaya
 When Salman called the film Wanted Khan, when the film was called Bodyguard, it was called Bodyguard, when the film was Dabangg, it was called Dabangg Khan

 salmaan khan ne apane parivaar kaa bharpoor khyaal rakhaa

 aise main zaahir he ki salmaan ko kisi na kisi kii dua lagegi hi

 Eid or Diwali, Navratri or Ganapati, celebrate all festivals
 salmaan khan samaaj seva se bhi pichley kai saalon se jude rahe hai
 an institution called Being Human through which the poor are supported
 garibon kaa ilaaj karte hai salmaan
 Salman Khan spends a large part of his hard-earned money to help the poor through Being Human
 zaahir he garibon kii awaz or dua sidhe bhagwaan ke paas pahunchati he jiskaa fal salmaan ko mil rahaa he, unki apaar safalata ke naam par
 Salman Khan achieved what he wished in his life, be it stardom, immense success at the box office, big fan following, family love, friends friendship, respect or the blessings of millions of fans
 
 
 vaaki kuch to baat he salmaan main, tabhi to wo sabakaa bhaijan he
 After that, Salman became one of the biggest stars of the 90s by giving successful films like 'andaz Apna Apna', 'karan Arjun', 'jeet', 'twins' and 'pyar Kiya To Darna Kya' and his rivals Aamir Khan And had made a different place for himself, competing Shahrukh Khan at the box office
 magar milinium kii shuruyaat salmaan ke liye khushgavaar nahin thi
 After the ascension of 2000, films like 'hum Tumhare Hain Sanam', 'har Dil Jo Pyaar Karega', 'tumko Na Bhoolgeon' and 'ye Hai Jalwa' flopped but Salman made a strong comeback with the film 'tere Naam'
 
 iske baad film 'garv', 'no entry', 'mujhase shaadi karogi' or 'partner' jaisi filmein lagaataar badi hit hoti chali gayi
 Once again a small phase came when the films 'jaane Mana', 'salaam e Ishq' and 'yuvraj' flopped, but Salman Khan's body was overturned in the 2008 film 'wanted'
 'wanted' ke baad film 'vir' haalanki safal nahin hui, lekin iske baad film 'dabang' se aisi safalata kii misaal banaai jo kismat waalon ko hi milti he
 After crossing the 100 crore collection from Dabangg, Salman Khan became a box office bully and after that all his films became super hits and grossed over 100 crores
 dabang ke baad 'bodyguard', 'ready', 'dabang2', 'jai ho' or 'ek tha tiger' jaisi sabhi filmon ne 100 karod se zyaada kaa aankada paar kiya
 After this, Salman also crossed the 200 crore mark at the box office with the film 'kick'
 ab film 'bajrangi bhaijan' aa rahi he or aisa lagata he ki ye film bhi 200 karod kaa aankada paar kar legi
 Salman Khan's big fan following made him stand on a different position
 salmaan ne jab-jab jo-jo kiya wo fishan ban gaya
 When Salman landed the shirt for the first time in the film Pyaar Kiya To Darna Kya, it became a fashion to take off the shirt in films
 yuvaaon ko acchhee body banane kaa josh bhi salmaan ne hi diya or salmaan ko hi dekhakar yuva body banane ke liye utar gaye or desh main gymnasium kaa chalan badha
 When Salman had long hair falling on his forehead in the film 'tere Naam', the youth adopted that hairstyle
 salmaan ne jab film wanted kii tab wanted khan kahalaaye, jab film body guard kii tab bodyguard kahalaaye, jab film dabang kii tab dabang khan kehalaae
 That is, they kept getting different titles from different films
 ab jab se film 'bajrangi bhaijan' ke promo shuru hue hai tab se salmaan 'bajrangi bhaijan' bhi kahalaane lage hai
 Salman Khan played all kinds of roles in his long film journey
 apane alag andaaz ke liye alag jagah banaai or alag tarah ke bindaas dance ke liye alag mukaam banaaya
 Salman Khan took great care of his family
 abhinay se kareeb-kareeb dur ho chuke apane bhai arbaz or sohail khan va jija atul agnihotri ko nirmaataa or nirdeshak banaaya
 Salman plays in his films and the film is a hit
 salmaan khan apane parivaar ke saath-saath dusron kii bhi khub sahaayta karte hai
 The credit for making music composer Himesh Reshammiya, sajid-wajid successful also goes to Salman
 katrina kaiff or sonakshi sinha ko bhi star salmaan ne hi banaaya he
 Salman is giving a chance to return to director Suraj Barjatya who has been failing for some time with the film 'prem Ratan Dhan Payo'
 aisi bahut sari misaalen hai jinke liye salmaan sahaara banakar khadey rahete hai
 In such a situation, it is obvious that Salman will have to pray for someone
 tippaniyan Salman respects all religions
 id ho yaa diwaali, navaratri ho yaa ganpati, sabhi tyoharon ko manaate hai
 Salman Khan has also been associated with social service for the last several years
 beeing human naam kii sanstha banaai he jiske dwaara garibon kii sahaayta hoti he
 Salman treats the poor
 apni mehnat kii kamai kaa bada hissaa salmaan khan beeing human ke madhyam se garibon kii sahaayta main lagaate hai
 It is obvious that the voice and blessings of the poor reach God directly, whose fruits are being paid to Salman, in the name of his immense success
 salmaan khan ne apane jivan main jo chaha hasil kiya, phir wo chaahe staradam ho, box offis par apaar safalata ho, badi fain folowing ho, parivaar kaa pyaar ho, doston kii dosti ho, sammaan ho yaa phir lakhon prashansakon kii dua

 com par bhi privet skulon dwaara fees badhotaree or anya tarah kii shikaayatein kii ja sakati hai

 The comments abhibhavakon kii ore se shikaayat milane ke baad dilli up-mukhyamantri or shiksha mantri manish sisodiya ne sakhti dikhaate hue buudhvaar shaam ko hi kalka public skool ko nirdesh jari karavaaya ki ve sarkaar se bina purv anumati ke fees na badhayen, anyathaa sarkaar kadai se nipategi
 In the midst of these developments, the Delhi government also decided to open a complaint center and issue an email to make a complaint
 edablyooes / diji admician main dhaandhlee, vittiya aniyamitata or teachers kaa farji record rakhane ke maamle saamne aane ke baad dilli sarkaar maiks fort skool kii do branch ko techover karne kaa notice thama chuki he
 According to the Delhi High Court order, schools which have got land from the government cannot increase the fees without the prior permission of the Delhi government
 kuch skulon ne fees badhaane ke liye dilli sarkaar se anumati maangi he lekin sarkaar ne abhi tak kisi bhi skool ko isaki anumati nahin di he
 In such a situation, if any school increases the fees, then the Delhi government can take action against it
 abhibhavak skulon kii manamaani sambandhi shikaayatein aasaani se kar saken, isliye ab sarkaar ne privet skool shikaayat centre khol diya he
 Also, arrangements have been made to complain through e-mail
 buudhvaar kii dopaher kareeb 150 abhibhavakon ne mukhyamantri awaas par dilli ke mukhyamantri arvind kejariwal or up-mukhyamantri manish sisodiya se mulaakaat karke alaknanda sthit kalka public skool dwaara fees badhaaye jane kii shikaayat kii thi
 After hearing the complaint, Chief Minister Arvind Kejriwal had said that the government has not allowed any school to increase the fees and they should not give the increased fees, they continue to pay the old fees
 tippaniyan After receiving the complaint from the parents, Delhi Deputy Chief Minister and Education Minister Manish Sisodia, sternly, issued instructions to the Kalka Public School on Wednesday evening not to increase the fees without prior permission from the government, otherwise the government will deal strictly
 inhen ghatnakram ke bich dilli sarkaar ne shikaayat centre kholane or shikaayat karne ke liye i-mail jari karne kaa bhi nirnay le liya

 is baar buddha poornima 18 may 2019 ko manaai ja rahi he
 Why Buddha Purnima is celebrated? When Lord Buddha learned about violence, sin and death in his life, he gave up his fascination and freed himself from his household life and went in search of the truth of life

 2
 is din buddha dharm ke maanane vaale log mathon main ikatthe hokar prarthana karte hai

 is din log buddha viharon or mathon ko rangeen jhandon se sajaate hai or buddha kii shikshaaon kaa jaap karte hai
 4
 is din buddha dharm ke log ghar or mandiron main bhagwaan buddha kii murti ke agarbatti or mombatiyaan jalaakar bhagwaan buddha se prarthana karte hai
 5
 is din garibon main kapade or khaanaa baanta jaataa he
